Daxia Middle School: Continues to Run Kindergarten Normal Department

Daxia University on Zhongshan Road in this city ran a kindergarten normal school in the autumn of 1930. The various facilities were quite large. Later, due to the January 28th Incident, the school was merged into the senior normal department of the attached Daxia Middle School. It is estimated that 28 students have graduated and are not idle, which shows that the society needs this kind of training urgently, and the school is suitable for training this kind of teacher. Now that the high school normal department is gradually coming to an end, and the society still urgently needs kindergarten teachers, the school has considerable equipment for this department. Therefore, it has submitted a request to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau to forward it to the Ministry of Education to approve the continuation of the kindergarten normal department in order to create more opportunities. It is reported that the school has received the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's instruction No. 236176 from the Ministry of Education approving the continuation. Therefore, it has been decided to enroll 50 new students (exclusively female) for the first semester during the summer vacation. The study period is set at three years. The admission qualification must be junior high school graduation, and a kindergarten is attached for practical teaching. It is reported that the school will continue to run the 8th summer school in order to use the summer time to expand educational efficiency. All important subjects in high and junior high school, such as Chinese, English, mathematics, science, chemistry, etc., will be selected to open classes. The kindergarten normal department and the summer school are preparing a brochure, and a stamped envelope will be sent upon request.

Publication of Modern Navigation

The Chinese Institute of Navigation is the only academic organization in the country that studies navigation. Since its establishment, it has made many contributions to the country and society. Now that there are more and more navigators, and most of the textbooks and reference books used are in foreign languages, scholars must spend a long time studying the language, but they have no time to study the scientific content in depth, resulting in more effort and less gain. This has long been a common problem in our country's education, and the slow progress of science has not been a major reason for this. The association, seeing this, publishes books on sailing techniques every year, intending to remedy this deficiency and facilitate scholars in our country who are interested in this. It is now heard that Yang Guanyuan, the chief editor of the association, has compiled a new Modern Navigation, which is based on new and practical materials. It is said that it has been inscribed and prefaced by famous Party-state figures and senior figures in navigation such as Hu Hanmin, Xu Jixiang, Ma Chaojun, Ouyang Ge, Wu Daming, Luo Panhui, and Zhang Zhijiang, which makes it even more impressive. The book has now been published, and major bookstores in this city are selling it.

Finance American Silver Policy Unchanged, Gold Standard Rises and Falls

Result of Lingering is Just a Small Triangle

The gold market initially rose and then fell yesterday. The market situation for half a day was extremely mediocre. The situation was stable in the middle. Both supply and demand lacked excitement. Foreign news reported that the US Treasury Secretary replied to the silver faction, saying that the government would continue to purchase silver and would not change its previous policy. The spot market also weakened, resulting in a slight setback. In the morning, the overseas silver market saw the British rise and the American shrink. The Monte Carlo forward silver price shrank, but not by much. Exchange rates all increased. London raw gold remained unchanged. Reports stated that a meeting of American silver faction congressmen was adjourned due to insufficient numbers and would be rescheduled. People's minds were still calm. Shanghai's pre-market trading opened at 71.x yuan. Major players entered the market, immediately pulling it up to 75.6 yuan before settling slightly. The Central Bank's listed prices were announced, with both British and American rising. Customs gold units fell by 1.1%. The gold standard price was lowered again to 841.5 yuan, causing it to trend downwards immediately after opening. Refined gold only increased by 11 yuan. Banks' appetites became increasingly blocked. HSBC's listed prices announced a rise of 125 for the British pound and 4.375 for the American dollar. Traders actively engaged in arbitrage, lacking support and retreating into the 70 yuan range. Buyers took advantage of the low prices to provide support, managing to pull it up. However, with the exchange market hardening and selling pressure intensifying, it was difficult to sustain. Foreign news reported that US Treasury Secretary Morgenthau had responded to inquiries from silver faction senators, saying that the government would not change its silver policy and would continue to purchase silver. This news coincided with HSBC's blocked sales, further breaking the 70 yuan mark. However, with limited trading, there was still support at the lower prices. It soon rose above 70 yuan, gradually recovering. Finally, the exchange market stabilized, and there was a lack of large supply and demand in the market, resulting in a calm market situation with narrow fluctuations. The final trend was flat with more consolidation. This is also what should have happened before the fall. I will now record the market situation for half a day.

Grain: Widespread Drought Causes Flour and Wheat Prices to Surge

The flour market yesterday saw another unanimous surge in prices during the morning. Although the quoted prices for foreign wheat in Chicago and Canada saw a slight decrease of eight fractional points, industry insiders remained indifferent. Initial price offerings remained stable, but due to the continued severe drought in various regions, sentiments in inland areas became uniformly bullish. Consequently, buying interest surged after the market opened, driving prices upwards, prompting further purchases. Inland buyers also actively joined the buying spree, causing near-term futures to jump by a significant three to four fractional points. By the afternoon opening, near-term futures experienced a slight correction as factories engaged in minor hedging sales, stabilizing market sentiment. However, long-term futures saw fewer short positions, leading to robust demand and a tense market situation. Towards the close, prices retreated by about one fractional point as leveraged positions were unwound. Despite the lack of specific causes for the current upward trend, it is feared that market sentiment will remain strong unless widespread rainfall arrives. As a result, the price for this month rose by 1.25%, July rose by 3.75%, August rose by 4.5%, September rose by 4.375%, October rose by 5%, and November rose by 5.5%.

Yesterday, the wheat futures market also saw a unanimous surge. Following the wheat harvest, the Jiangnan and Jiangbei regions continue to suffer from severe drought. The great drought and massive disasters of last year remain fresh in memory. If sufficient rainfall does not arrive, public anxiety will inevitably escalate. The market was relatively stable in July, but the surge in the flour market triggered a sudden surge in buying interest, driving prices higher. General inland customers, witnessing this situation, dared not engage in excessive hedging, leading to demand exceeding supply and a continuous rise in prices. By the afternoon opening, market sentiment remained positive, and prices continued to rise by three to four fractional points. Subsequently, long positions were unwound, leading to a slight decline. As a result at closing, July futures rose by a significant 12 fractional points, August rose by 7 fractional points, September rose by 9 fractional points, and October rose by 11 fractional points. The current wheat market, due to the significant increase in standard wheat prices, cannot be ignored and has also seen a price increase of two to three fractional points. The market remains strong, with an estimated volume of over 5,000 bags. Henan old wheat was quoted at 3.45 yuan, Wuyi new wheat at 3.40 yuan, Daqiao Zhenjiang wheat at 3.34 yuan, Gaozi Puzhen Yangzhou wheat at 3.30 yuan, Mingguang wheat at 3.44 yuan, Zhitang Penglai wheat at 3.27 yuan, Danyang wheat at 3.30 yuan (second grade 3.27 yuan), Taicang wheat at 3.24 yuan, Anting wheat at 3.26 yuan, Jiading wheat at 3.16 yuan, Kunshan wheat at 3.26 yuan. Fuxin sold 3,200 bags, and Fufeng, Xinda, and Shenda collectively sold 1,700 bags.

Regarding the proposal to abolish the Winnipeg Grain Exchange for Chicago wheat, opposition is strong, and it is unlikely to be implemented. Estimated yields for the current winter and spring wheat harvests are approximately 67 million bushels, which is generally considered a substantial amount.

Erratic Rainfall Causes Continued Rise in Foreign Rice Prices, While Du Geng Rice Remains Stable

The foreign rice market continued to show firm and active trading yesterday. Due to uneven rainfall and widespread drought, particularly in the Jiangzhe interior, where drought disasters occurred last year, anxieties are heightened this year. Although there was no continued handling of Yangtze River shipments, inland demand was more active, and local merchants continued to fulfill orders. The market atmosphere remained tense, and Saigon No. 3 rice was sought after by local and Jiangzhe inland buyers, with prices rising by five fractional points. Shipments also remained buoyant. If strong demand continues and there is no widespread rain, rice prices are bound to rise again. Over 10,000 bags of Saigon rice were sold throughout the day, along with 60 bags each of Xiao Jiaoluo rice, and 745 bags of Ke Xian rice, with inland areas remaining the primary destination.

Local rice (South Shanghai) saw a total of 30 shipments yesterday (nearly 1,000 shi). Local sales were sluggish, and orders were not being fulfilled, causing the overall market to soften. South Hong Kong early rice prices fell, while other late rice varieties were also lower. Only Su Tong Geng rice remained stable due to limited supply. The yin bian yuan variety remained unaffected. (North Shanghai) 16 or 17 boats arrived from various river areas yesterday. Market demand remained weak, but sellers were reluctant to sell cheaply due to the drought. White Geng rice prices turned firmer again, while White Yuan and dry rice varieties stabilized. Prices for various grades of rice remained largely unchanged.

Shen Bao Guohuo (National Products) Weekly

Effective Methods for Students to Use National Products

— Pan Jiayu

It is universally known that citizens should use national products. How can students, as representatives of the intellectual class, not do their best to promote their use? There are indeed reasons for this, which can be stated as follows:

(1) Many lower-level students are unable to discern whether goods are national products or foreign goods.

(2) Unethical merchants often falsely claim that foreign goods are national products.

(3) Some are unaware that there are similar national products to certain foreign goods.

(4) Some overlook the importance of national products because of the temporary lower prices of foreign goods.

The reasons are as stated above, specifically the deception of unscrupulous merchants and the negligence of the students themselves. Therefore, students' failure to fully utilize national products should not be immediately labeled as "unpatriotic." It is truly because the methods of promoting national products have not been perfected and made effective.

The so-called effective methods are not mere empty talk but concrete measures implemented in practice. To avoid the above four issues, one must prevent students from being deceived and ensure that they can confirm that the goods they use are national products. To achieve this, there must be an organized and systematic student joint consumer cooperative. I will now present my tentative ideas, outlining the organization and methods, as a reference for implementation.

This cooperative must be proactively formed by students or supported by national product trade organizations. It can start with one school initiating the process, inviting representatives from various schools to organize preparatory matters. Then, student self-governing associations from middle schools and above can elect committee members, and lower-level schools can appoint teachers as committee members to jointly organize the committee to handle the process. At the same time, a supervisory committee is also formed to oversee the committee's work.

The responsibility of this committee is to organize consumer cooperatives, adopting a trust-like agency system but without charging commissions. On the one hand, it connects with honest and trustworthy merchants or manufacturers to conduct trade with the most suitable prices and the most reliable national products. On the other hand, it properly handles the application of goods needed by students. The so-called student application goods can be divided into three categories: stationery, clothing, and other supplies. We will now discuss each of these categories separately based on their nature:

(1) Stationery: Stationery is used by students at all times, and its consumption is the largest, so the potential for waste is also the greatest. However, it is very difficult to distinguish whether it is a foreign product or a national product, because foreign products using "Made in China" are countless, making it impossible to determine. Furthermore, the prices are mostly not expensive, and sometimes buyers easily overlook them and do not investigate deeply. Now, to promote national stationery, we can reform the school's inherent small store. The students of each school can gather shares to establish a fund to purchase the required stationery. The purchased goods must be inspected by the cooperative committee, and a resident committee member can be assigned to each school to investigate or report.

(2) Clothing: If we seek to use only national products for student clothing materials, it will be difficult to carry out in practice because the clothing materials of various students are generally different. Therefore, to encourage the use of national products, implementing a school uniform system is the only solution. The committee of this cooperative can first send a letter to the school authorities, agreeing to act as an agent. The school authorities select the color, material, and price range, and then the committee properly selects the most economical and high-quality national products for students to purchase and wear uniformly.

(3) Other Supplies: Other application items such as artistic and technical application items, such as cameras and printing machines, can also be handled by the cooperative. However, the method is slightly different. First, the requesting buyer submits a purchase request (specifying the name, type, style, and price range of the item) to the committee, applying for purchase and paying a corresponding deposit. The committee agrees to deliver it within a few days, and then the remaining payment is paid to collect the goods.

If the above three items can be implemented, the effectiveness will be considerable, and there are three benefits:

First, in principle, it can promote national products.

Second, in practice, students can save money economically.

Third, the success of this organization can provide students with good practical experience and strengthen the relationship between students, cultivating a sense of unity.

Three Things that Chinese People Should Pay Attention to

— Pan Yishi

Another year has easily passed, and half of the twenty-fourth year is already over. This year was designated as the Student National Products Year. The scene of representatives from various schools swearing to use national products is still vividly like in front of my eyes. This publication has carried many articles on promoting national products. On the whole, I think the results will not repeat the mistakes of the Women's National Products Year!

Because students are young and promising, energetic young people, with knowledge and enthusiasm. Therefore, the implementation effect will not disappoint people too much, but there are a few points that we should pay special attention to, and I specifically bring them up for discussion.

First, shift the aesthetic concept. Generally speaking, Chinese people have a common problem, that is, they think that foreign-made things are all good. For example, if someone asks A where he bought this item, A will definitely answer that it was from large companies such as Huila or Wing On. Only in this way can he show his generosity. This kind of malpractice is wrong. Not only should we not glorify extravagance, but we don't need to blindly believe in foreign goods. We should take simplicity as the main thing. For everything in daily life, we only seek spiritual comfort and pleasure. There is no need to care about the material enjoyment and satisfaction. We should be proud of buying national products. Everyone unanimously resists foreign goods, even if foreign goods desperately come to dump them and take over our own business market?

Second, discard the concept of vanity, and develop the habit of seeking truth from facts. Most people are delayed by vanity all their lives, to the point of being irreparable. Not only are rights lost, but even the country is destroyed and the family is destroyed. This is a big reason. From now on, we should discard vanity and put this spirit into the welfare of the country, so that we can solve any difficult things.

Third, act with conscience. Most people hang a sheep's head and sell dog meat. On the surface, they speak thoughtfully. We should love the country, promote national products, and restore rights and interests. But in reality? I am still a salesman for foreign goods, and indirectly selling out the country. It is absolutely wrong to bury my conscience like this.

If we can pay attention to the above three points and work hard to do it, I don't think it will take ten years. I guarantee that the country will be rich and the people will be strong, and the impact of any recession will not invade our territory again.

The Weekly Meeting of the Nanjing National Products Company

— Shi Ming

——The Significance Is Worth Emulating——

Nanjing National Products Company. Opened on the Double Tenth Festival last year. Business is very developed. At the beginning of its establishment. Former Mayor Shi Ying was appointed as chairman of the board. Shi held himself with integrity and honesty. He usually wears cloth clothes and coarse clothes. Dedicated to promoting national products. Therefore, You Le helped it succeed. Manager Ge Liangchou. Smart and capable. Very serious about doing things. Outstanding achievements in internal management. As a result, the business is booming.

To want the development and success of a career in the business world. The first. It is solid in the proper management. The so-called calculated win. Careful planning. Must be careful at all times. Catch up. Make the goods sold not miss the timeliness. Turnover is easy to circulate. Then it will be of help. Second. It is in the appropriate personnel management. No management means no plan. And management is too strict. Lost in rigidness. There is no vitality. Too lax. It is easy to become licentious. Affect the job. To be tolerant and strict. Both rigid and soft. It is in the manager's ability to have the knowledge of the times. Recognize the business itself and the environment. Deal with it with a dedicated spirit. Adapt to circumstances without harming the business. That's almost it.

Nanjing National Products Company. There is one point worth mentioning in terms of personnel management. Every Tuesday morning at 7:30 a.m. (the company usually opens for business at 8:30 a.m.). The manager convenes all employees. Hold weekly talks on the second floor. The scope of the talks is to develop business and promote the spirit of patrol service. Including merchants' ethics and youth's advanced studies. Any kind of national product that is sluggish in sales. Any kind that caters to the needs. I will also discuss it from time to time. Participating employees. You can express your opinions. To eliminate barriers. A gathering to blend feelings. To dissect the essence of the matter. Rational judgment. To seek the promotion of one's own business. This kind of approach. The meaning is really commendable. Mr. Ge said that the business world is most afraid of the manager and employees. Each is due to the relationship in status. Do not talk to each other. It's like dividing the Hongtao. To affect the effectiveness of service. Leading to intangible losses. Human resources are not reduced. It's really sighable. Mr. Wan has gained this kind of experience. Continuing to generate legitimate management. At the same time, he sets an example everywhere. Words and deeds are consistent. Business prospects. Naturally, it will be promoted in order.

The times are evolving. Commercial knowledge must be adequately equipped. So that you can deal with it with ease. In today's world, to be the leader of an industry. Then how to complete the conditions for this leader's qualifications. Make the industry successful and the matter belongs. It's a prerequisite issue. The author is by no means using private superficial views. Boasting about Mr. Wan's strengths. Only with Nanjing National Products Company. As a giant of the capital's commerce. The meaning of his weekly meeting is enough to facilitate management. It is beneficial to both the body and mind. It seems that it can be used as a model for the national business community. It is not harmful to spread it. Finally, I hope that those who follow the example will pay attention. If you also hold weekly talks. Its motivation should be to connect feelings and exchange opinions. Fortunately, do not make it like the speech of an official. It would be boring and lose its meaning.

Creed of Promoting National Products

— Zhen

Wearing national products is a pure expression of our national citizens.

Eating national products is the source of strength for our national citizens.

Using national products is the savings of money for our national citizens.

Sitting in national product boats and vehicles is an expression of healthy travel for our national citizens.

Promoting national products is the basis for the economic independence of our national citizens.

Promoting national products is the only weapon for our national citizens to use against the outside world.

Government offices and schools using national products are examples for national citizens to promote.

Making efforts to use national products ourselves is the absolute obligation of our national citizens.

Making efforts to have our families use national products is the inherent responsibility of our national citizens.

Making efforts to persuade our friends to use national products is the natural duty of our national citizens.

Thoughts After the Bankruptcy of the Shanghai National Products Company

— Zhang Mengzhao

Over the past Dragon Boat Festival, unfortunate bad news continued to come! The Shanghai National Products Company, which has made considerable efforts in the national products sector, has actually been reported to have gone bankrupt! This cannot but make people sigh! I feel a painful thing - when foreign goods are dumped - invading the mainland urgently! The front line of my national products sector has shaken again, isn't it over? Indeed, the National Products Company owes money to creditors, and the holiday season has arrived, which cannot be taken lightly, but owing money is a small matter, and destroying a well-known national products agency, damaging the original energy of the national products sector! Affect the entire business market! Cut off the livelihood of workers! Increasing the number of unemployed in society is even more serious!

Secondly: the shareholders who founded the National Products Company, and the managers who presided over the national products business, should reflect on themselves; first, they should concentrate on the planning of the business and not hold other positions at the same time; second, they should work hard with all their energy and down-to-earth, how to promote national products, how to strictly employ people, how to tighten expenses, and how to consolidate the economy, holding calculations and plans every evening! Where else can you put your heart on foreign affairs?

Mr. Wu Zhijun's boldness! We should admire, but his concurrent positions are not specialized, scattered and unplanned, and meaningless exaggeration! Not seeking practical enrichment! Is his big disease! The car overturned in front, the car behind the mirror! Those who operate the national products business, do they know how to be frightened and vigilant?

A Record of Visiting the Wenguang Brand Carbon Paper Factory

— Qin Xi

One day, I went to the stationery section of a certain bookstore to buy carbon paper. The clerk asked, "Do you want foreign carbon paper or Chinese carbon paper?" I was very surprised to hear this. Carbon paper, I thought, was only imported. Could there be a Chinese version? At that time, I told the clerk that I wanted Chinese carbon paper. He took out a box for me to look at. I saw that the outside of the box was dark blue, and the front of the box had the words "Please Use Domestic Goods, Wenguang Brand Carbon Paper, Shanghai Wenguang Craft Company." I was very excited to take out the carbon paper to observe, but the surface was just so-so. Fortunately, the price was only seventy cents in silver dollars, so I bought a box and took it home to try. Wow! It was really good. Carefully checking the description inside the box, I learned that the Wenguang Craft Company was located in Huiyuan Lane, Huade Road, Shanghai.

Although I am not a twelve or thirteen-year-old child, my curiosity is stronger than anyone else's. How is carbon paper made? I wanted to know a little about it. So, last Saturday afternoon, taking advantage of having nothing to do, I took the number 10 bus to visit the Wenguang Craft Company. The company was in the second alley of Huiyuan Lane, and there was an enamel sign on the door that read "Factory Restricted Area, No Admittance." It was inconvenient to knock on the door and go in. However, next to the door of the neighboring house, there was another enamel sign that read "Wenguang Craft Company," so I raised my hand and knocked on the brass ring. In less than a minute, an elderly man of about fifty years old came out and invited me in, asking what was the matter. I took out a business card and explained that I had come specifically to visit the factory. He did not refuse and even expressed a welcoming tone. After exchanging pleasantries, he led me to take a look around. I saw that the factory was steaming with heat, and a dozen or so workers were working hard. The following Q&A is the little bit of new knowledge I gained:

(Question) When was your company founded?

(Answer) It was initiated in October of the 23rd year of the Republic of China (1934), and opened on December 1st of the same year.

(Question) What is your company's capital, how many shareholders are there, and is it a company in nature?

(Answer) The capital is only a few thousand dollars, there are only four or five shareholders, and in fact, it can be called a limited partnership.

(Question) Was this manufacturing method learned from abroad, or was it invented by yourself?

(Answer) Foreign carbon paper manufacturing uses very complex printing machines. These machines are very expensive, and we don't have much capital, so we are temporarily using manual labor. When we expand in the future, we must use machines. However, the current manual manufacturing is the result of much research.

(Question) What raw materials are used to make carbon paper? Can you tell me where these raw materials come from?

(Answer) We use many kinds of raw materials, such as stearin, paraffin, kanshan, drying oil, sodium carbonate, etc., too many to list. Some of these things are purchased from Western pharmacies, and some are purchased from raw material stores. However, we absolutely avoid buying inferior goods, and this can be testified to by Heaven and Earth.

(Question) Then, there are many inferior goods of popular paper types on the market. Can you avoid them all?

(Answer) This can be proved by the brand on the colored leather. If you don't believe it, please come to the office and I will show you the evidence.

Speaking of which, we returned to the previous room. He took out a package of paper from the drawer and picked out many paper brand signs, such as Czechoslovakian brands, German Baibeiles Paper Factory brands, and various logos of Liu Hai Trading Company of Han Kee Foreign Firm, managed by Norway. I am a layman when it comes to paper, but after this conversation, I realized that the paper mills in Western countries are indeed very great. As I was about to ask more questions, the telephone on the wall rang loudly. I thanked him and left.

A Week of New Information from the Domestic Goods Industry

Textile expert Mr. Wei Xudong spent three years successfully creating ramie yarn. He plans to establish the China Ramie Textile Company to specialize in manufacturing it. Industry leaders Rong Zongjing and Guo Shun have already testified to this.

The Ministry of Industry recently plans to set up paper mills and silk factories to plug huge financial leaks.

Various merchant groups in this city held a joint meeting on the 7th and decided to establish the Singapore Chinese Chamber of Commerce National Exhibition. The preparatory office is located in the City Chamber of Commerce exhibition hall, and many guidelines for the process were passed.

The Commodity Inspection Bureau of the International Trade Bureau sent separate letters to domestic goods manufacturers in Shanghai, Ping, Jin, Min, and other places, soliciting products to participate in the Belgian Commodity Exhibition Hall. They are to be sent to the National Trade Bureau by the end of this month and shipped to Belgium in early July.

The Zhenru District Student Domestic Goods Exhibition, sponsored by the Student Domestic Goods Promotion Association, opened on the 10th at Jinan University.

Tianjin and Changsha recently plan to prepare for domestic goods exhibitions. Mr. Qi Shao'an, director of the Tianjin Domestic Goods Exhibition Hall, has come to Shanghai to discuss the matter.

Since its opening, the Domestic Goods City in this city has been doing very well. Every day, many people come to the city to shop and visit. The Shanghai National Products Company, which was forced to close due to the collapse of the Ningbo Industrial Bank, may be re-opening soon. Unemployed employees sent a letter to Mr. Ren Jinpin, inviting enthusiastic domestic goods leaders to find a way to resume operations.

The Dutch East Indies has banned the import of Chinese medicinal wines since July 1st.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Linghu Zhao)

Strictly speaking, "a person's life" is nothing more than "birth, old age, sickness, and death." If you want to discuss all the relationships between individuals and the country and society, whether you are doing great national salvation work or trivial neighborhood affairs, you must lay the foundation of common knowledge around the age of twenty!

Otherwise, when you are nearly forty or fifty years old and your brainpower is weakening, it will be too late to lay the foundation of common knowledge, isn't it?

To be honest, when we reach forty or fifty years old, when Confucius said we are "not to be feared," how can our blood and energy be as strong as when we were young? At this time, the goal is only to do "old age, sickness, and death" work. In fact, to be frank, this work is nothing more than trying to make some money for the future!

A Pile of Walls (Part 1)

— Rong Yu

When I see the four characters "Clean Wall Movement" on this paper, a pile of walls that are commonly seen on the streets of our country will appear in my mind.

Originally, it was a very good pile of walls, but it was damaged and soiled by the wind, rain, and moss, which was unavoidable. However, our walls, which were brand new a few days ago, have been decorated with all kinds of artificial coatings, becoming a bizarre ancient painting; and they fully show all kinds of evil roots.

Clearly written are the four large characters "Posting Prohibited," but above them, the glittering and brilliant theater previews and store discount sales advertisements are densely plastered with a thick layer, which can even be used as a mat. Below it is written, "Urination Prohibited, Violators Will Be Arrested," or a very large tortoise is painted, but the yellow urine stains at the foot of the wall and the pungent smell are like a sign to attract urination. The above two facts tell people about the bad habit of "knowingly violating public morals."

Also! On narrow red strips of paper, it is written "Selling Severe Cold - See Immediate Results," or "Heaven Yellow, Earth Yellow, My Family Has a Crying Child, Kind Gentlemen, Recite Once and Sleep Through the Night." This kind of witchcraft and harmful-to-others-but-not-beneficial-to-oneself tone fully demonstrates the lack of common sense among the people.

Red and green posters with the words "×× Hall Guarantees Treatment of Syphilis and Gonorrhea" also occupy the central position of the wall, which indicates the phenomenon of "prostitution is rampant, nine out of ten are sick."

Street urchins, with nothing to do, also draw rough lines and misshapen models on the walls; they also write slogans such as "×× Little Five Cars ×× Ten Bones," which can also indicate our social education and children's education.

Such walls, standing on the streets, are truly laughable and tearful to appreciate carefully!

A Record of Tea Tasting in the Summer House

— Huo Xueming

On the day before the Beginning of Summer, I visited the dwelling of Old Man Zao Fen. It was noon, and we had a meal together. The clear sun filled the empty courtyard, the clouds were fixed, and there was no wind. After drinking a little wine, my limbs felt soft, and we agreed to take a nap like Zai Yu. When I woke up, the setting sun was hanging on the eaves. I watched two white rabbits fighting for vegetable leaves: their eyes were like red rubies, they lifted their long ears, and their cheeks moved quickly. I felt very comfortable. Suddenly, I thought of tea, which would write of leisure. Then I remembered Xia Yizi, whom I hadn't seen for two years. He hangs his teapot on Beijing Road, selling both tea and inkpad; and he is still the tea emperor dominating Shanghai. At this time, Uncle Fan also arrived, so the three of us went straight to Xia's house. After a short while, Yizi came out and shook hands with us, talking loudly. The four of us, in a space that was neither elegant nor vulgar, sat around a square table, cleaned the teapot and plates, and rinsed the cups and dishes. First, we tried "Ming Qian." Yizi has been working with tea for many years, and his skills are like a doctor's. He showed his unique skills, dripping tea into the tea plate, so full that it did not overflow. Before it reached the nose, a clear fragrance had already arrived; before it reached the lips, saliva was already being produced. From this, I knew that the water must have come from Hupao; and the tea-producing place must be in Shifeng. The wax spring of Hupao can be sealed and stored for three years without spoiling; the leaves of Shifeng are as long as a flag and a spear; even if there is a slight difference, it is still credible. Then we tried "Lotus Flower," which was warm, rich, and lingered on the jaw. It was like being in a riverside pavilion after the rain, quietly facing the new lotus, the jade ring was silent, and the stream guest felt sad. I gazed into the distance, thinking of the center of the Wan River. Where else should I be buried? Finally, we tasted "Wild Tea," which came from Qinghai. Only two or three catties are harvested each year, because no medicine-gathering old man ties a rope and flies into the sky, exhausting the highest and most mysterious places, so it cannot be obtained. Its color is red, its taste is mellow, sweet and tough. It can be steeped twenty or thirty times, and the taste does not change much, and the color does not fade much. I guess it grows on dangerous peaks, receiving much of the essence of frost and dew, so it is so magical! We tasted a total of three varieties, two tastings of each: "Ming Qian" was round, "Lotus Flower" was sharp, and "Wild Tea" was broad. However, making tea is really difficult to describe: it must be accurate in weight and temperature, and the timing must be precise. Therefore, even if you get Yunyu Phoenix Claws and cook Hupao spring water, if it is not in Yizi's hands, the taste will not be pure, and without Yizi to match, the comments will not be elegant; if you taste it without the right person, then even if it is beautiful, you will not fully understand its meaning. If Guanzhi hears this, he should not think it is irrelevant?

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 14: Another Kind of Understanding: Westerners Talk About Construction, Not Without Regrets; Seven Kinds of Lovesickness

You Rong said: There is no mistake in helping them with this matter. Poor people have their own poor calculations. If Wang Jun really marries this girl, perhaps he has a way. As for that girl, she can endure hardship and is hardworking, I guarantee there will be no problem. Zhichang saw him holding the hem of his long gown with both hands, lifting one foot and stepping on the stool, striking a very heroic pose. There is no need to describe that excitement. He then laughed: I am really in a difficult position. If I help him with this marriage, in fact, I feel it is not right. I oppose it, right? Mr. Zhou is so enthusiastic. You Rong said: Originally! You are a boss in Little Western Paradise, and you are so considerate and thoughtful to him, of course, there is a possibility of getting close. Wang Jun's suspicion is also within the bounds of human emotion. But in my eyes, I would not think like that, because you have great interests in mind, and even if you live in Xi'an for a few days, you do many things. Precisely because I do not suspect Mr. Cheng, I boldly advise Mr. Cheng to make it happen. Mr. Cheng, what do you think of my idea? Saying this, he looked at Zhichang with a smile. This made Zhichang not know what to say. He scratched his head and laughed, "You seem to be using a trick to encourage me. But since you are so enthusiastic, I will reluctantly follow your wishes. When the North Sea dries up, I will sound him out." Only then did Zhou You Rong put down his leg, lower his sleeves, and bow to him. (238)

Imperial Incense Drifting Record

— Originally written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

How beautiful is the scenery on the lake! The water is as clear as jade, and we can see all the way to the bottom of the lake from the boat. The lotus stalks that have not yet emerged from the water are easy to count one by one. People stare at the lake water for a long time, and their eyes suddenly feel several times brighter. Especially moving are the five-colored goldfish raised in the lake, which often wag their tails and pass through the green waves, like a line of red silk: some of the larger ones can even jump out of the water, making crisp, soft sounds and round ripples.

The sunlight shines impartially on our bodies, filling us with a vibrant vitality, and everyone forgets all worries and sufferings, preparing to enjoy themselves to the fullest. At that time, the palaces built by Wantao happened to be right in front of us. Looking at them from the boat in the distance, they were like the immortal mountains and pavilions depicted in novels.

The flowers and trees in the Summer Palace are originally very abundant, especially along the lake, there are especially many; tall, short, woody, herbaceous, there are really countless. From the boat, we can vaguely see them rising and falling in the bright sunlight with the wind, and at the same time, the fragrant flowers are constantly released because of their rising and falling. Occasionally blowing into our nostrils, there is a real feeling of refreshing the heart and spleen. (338)

The Last Lesson

— Ms. Fuji

I once read a French novel by the famous writer Daudet, translated by Hu Shi, "The Last Lesson." I felt that it depicted a cowardly elementary school student's patriotism in a profound and ironic way. It was much more interesting than those novels with patriotic themes that were laid out in a straightforward way. It wrote about the German soldiers pressing the border, and after the war was settled, this elementary school student realized that his past neglect and truancy when he could study his national language was wrong, and once he woke up, he wanted to turn to a book of his national language, but it was forbidden by others and impossible.

Because the last resort of a dead country is to destroy the culture of the country being destroyed, so that its history can be completely forgotten, permanently sinking, and unable to transcend. Such a poisonous trick, when you read the novel, you will still be indignant, and you will have more vigilance in your heart.

This announcement on the paper is still not popular. After watching the new film directed by Shen Xiling, "Nostalgia," there is also an interlude of "The Last Lesson," which makes me realize that its power is above Daudet's novel!

Foreign aggression is frequent, is it time to wake up? I hope everyone can watch this "Last Lesson" in the film, on the one hand, they can be alert to themselves, and on the other hand, they can also compare it with Daudet's novel to see who has the advantage in terms of artistic position. Fortunately, the screening of "Nostalgia" will probably not be too late.

Pinghua Dream

— (Made in a Boat on Yushan Mountain) Old Man Mingshan

Where is the clear stream and green water? Pinghua piles up and opens golden coins, with several houses leaning against the mountain and facing the stream. In the house, it is as if they are tuning the ice string. When the door opens, a golden bell rings, and suddenly good news falls from the sky. A good son and a good son-in-law come out to greet him (referring to Tu Cen and his eldest daughter Suye), holding hands and asking if they are well. The jade-like snow that has just been weaned from the breast is the granddaughter of the famous mountain. The gold and stone in the room are worth a lot of money. Not a single word is lost from the Qiyang drum. My son's study of seal script is even more refined, with a clear and leisurely artistic conception and a ancient and渾厚气. The five-foot-high attic behind the house, with white cranes coming and going from time to time on the eaves. The green Xiaohua dust-free does not open the seal, and it will be left for Mingshan to live in in the future.

World News

Japanese Graves

— Jiyun

The Japanese people are popular for cremation, and the ashes are placed in a wooden box and buried under a stone tower, so it does not take up much land. There are very few private graves, and most of them are buried in the open space near the temple. There are many temples in Japan, just like in our country, they have occupied all the famous mountains and scenery. There is a lot of open space on the mountains, which is used as a public cemetery. And the Japanese people all believe in Buddhism, so the temples have become their cemeteries.

The shape of the stone tower is very similar to the Mongolian Lama Tower, completely made of granite. It is more than ten feet high, and the stone base is about six feet square, with two or three steps. A cube-shaped stone block is placed on top, and then a round pillar of two or three feet high, the top of which is the square top of the tower, shaped like the top mark of a pagoda in our country, is carved from a whole piece of stone. The name, age, date of birth and death of the deceased are engraved on the round pillar. Men are called Jushi, and women are called Big Sister, which means good men and good women in our country. The ashes are hidden under the tower and are not easily exposed. There are also two or three people buried in one tower together, mostly brothers and sisters who died young. They do not have the custom of husband and wife being buried together in the same cave.

If you pay attention to the tomb, you can spend a few more dollars to buy a larger plot of land. Stone railings are built around the stone tower. There are also Kumen and stone gates and sills built in front of the tomb. In short, the things on the tombs of the Japanese people in the past were all made of stone. Now there have been improvements, using iron gates and fences. Stone towers are also made of artificial stone, but not many.

The graves of the middle class and below are only three or four feet high. Some can't even afford to build a stone tower. A small monument stands on a Huai Fang stone. The poorest of the poor, a root of white wood square column is inserted on the tomb, with the name written on it. Recently, as the public cemetery system in our country has gradually been promoted, they also have a public charnel house with the same meaning as a public cemetery. A large stone tower is built in the temple, and countless ashes can be placed underneath. The required price is more comfortable and cheaper than buying a tomb.

On the ground in front of the stone tower, there are also stone-made incense burners and candlestick stands. There are also stone vases for inserting Western flowers. The descendants often come to offer flowers, pray, and burn incense candles, but not often.

The tombs of the royal family and nobles are of course very different. The Nongchuan Family Temple in Shiba Park represents everything. The Tokugawa shogunate once acted as regent, and later returned it to the Japanese Emperor, and even now the descendants are still sealed as Dukes. The Japanese people admire Tokugawa and the Japanese Emperor the same. The family temple is very large, built on the mountain, divided into three layers. It is completely ancient Chinese architecture, probably similar to the architecture of the Ming Dynasty in our country.

The outermost is the Tang Gate, fully engraved with three-dimensional flowers, plants, mountains and rivers. Inside the gate there is a horizontal corridor, wooden wall, and also delicate carvings, like the carved short walls in our country's gardens. Directly opposite is the hall where the Baidian is built. Although it is not tall, it is brilliantly painted and extremely luxurious. Further inside, after passing the passage, is the Xiang Hall where portraits are hidden. The gold-lacquered shrine and the ancient offerings are arranged like a shrine or ancestral hall in our country. Behind the hall, at the top of the stone steps, is the stone tower for storing bones, which is similar to ordinary ones and is not very particular. There are a total of six or seven such palaces, enshrining the descendants of Tokugawa.

On the open space outside the hall, there are bell towers and ablution halls, facing each other on the left and right. Stone lanterns and copper lanterns are arranged on both sides, totaling more than a thousand. They are all carved with dragons and phoenixes, and the project is very large. The high and sloping roof is covered with green copper tiles. The doors and beams are all floating carvings of dragon and phoenix cloud heads. Plum blossoms, orchids, bamboos, chrysanthemums, and mountain rocks are just like Chinese paintings. Other things like the wooden pillars of Panji, painted with vermilion lacquer, depicting full-color patterns, and murals of lions and beauties. Everything is similar to the architecture of the Forbidden City in our country. Beautiful clothes, I am afraid that the tombs and mausoleums of the Japanese people are nothing more than this.

Page 17

Free Talk

Profoundity and Novelty

— Long Gonggong

In the Free Talk on June 6th, Mr. Wu wrote an article called "Rot and Abuse," opposing people who write articles using clichéd and abusive language. Although this opinion is not new, it is very good. But under the same theme, he fiercely attacked "putting effort into fixed sentences," attacking "deliberately writing," attacking "refusing to take the ordinary path," attacking "profoundity" and "novelty," which is really a bit strange.

There are at least two kinds of clichéd and abusive language commonly expressed in articles. The first is the corruption and abuse in thinking, and the second is the corruption and abuse in writing. Let's think about it: if there is nothing worth contributing to the reader in the article, and it only takes a hundred words to write an article for a lifetime, "superficial" is right, "ordinary" is right, and "fresh" is also very "fresh," but what help has he given to mankind? As for the corruption and abuse in writing, there are also two kinds: those seen in modern Chinese are naturally "trembling heartstrings," "pilgrimage," "scenic line," and "eyelids," while those seen in classical Chinese are "not only this," "pick up," "thorn hairpin cloth skirt," "unique style," "swords drawn and bows bent," etc.; and terms such as "institution," "architecture," "contradiction," and "trend" have their own scientific meanings. They will never be corrupt and abusive.

I oppose high-mindedness because it is hypocritical and divorced from reality; but I also oppose vulgarity because it is cowardly and often hinders the footsteps of reality. What forms the backbone of this vulgarity is "generalism." For a long, long time, generalism has been linked to the old problems of the Chinese people. Speaking vague and floating words, only touching the surface of everything and thinking that they already understand, writing articles without any real description or accurate judgment, always living a life of humor, funny, and frivolous ridicule, turning serious things into comic relief, calling serious things stupid, and calling difficult things stupid—this is the essence of generalism. For such people, there is not a day of sweating profusely, and even if there is, they have to change it to "not gasping for breath, not changing face." In short, everyone is like an official in the late Qing Dynasty, saying that a major event is "easy," but the result is not doing it.

Without unique insights, you cannot write a thesis, and without unique observations, you cannot write a creation. This uniqueness, because the reader has not thought about it, is profound; because the reader has not seen it, it is novel. When an author wants to express the unique and truly valuable things that he has grasped, he has to put effort into every word and sentence, and deliberately express it in the most appropriate, most precise, and most powerful way, and refuse to be clever and lazy, muddling through and letting it be ruined by superficial and weak敷衍. We do not think authors should be mocked, but rather the mockers themselves should be mocked.

Without knowing the truth of art, without demanding the deepening of the theme, and without seeing the complexity of reality, there will never be a good work.—What are you still saying about greatness?

As far as I can see, all the clichéd and abusive language is probably hidden in smooth-tongued and ordinary articles, written by vulgar and general writers who specialize in catering to the reader's shortcomings. These writers often give readers "a little easy fun," making them comfortable, not feeling any difficulty, and also "gaining nothing." If you want to find examples, please pay attention to the long serial novels in the newspaper.

Mr. Wuai's article only explains the difficulties and jokes that a Chinese person with no language education and a simple mind encounters when using nouns, verbs, adverbs, and various clauses, which has nothing to do with "corruption and abuse."

If we do not want our culture to forever remain at the stage of children's games and childishness, let us hope that every writer reaches the realm of profundity and novelty, we have been ordinary readers for long enough.

In the Carriage

— Yao Mu

—Random Jottings from the Mundane World, No. 2—

Friend,

I trust you have received my first letter? "Is it a dream or madness?" you might be thinking, my friend. But understand, one newly awakened from a nightmare, his murmurings are at least akin to nonsensical ramblings!

I am now comfortably seated in a first-class carriage. I am still my free self—free as Sun Wukong returning to the Water Curtain Cave after Tang Sanzang was eaten by demons and the group temporarily disbanded. After rubbing my drowsy eyes several times, I can pick out some true and real things I have seen and heard along the way to tell you.

After sleeping soundly through the night, the scenery along the way has changed to the flavor of the north. —The dry plains of Guanghan, the hot wind blowing yellow dust, the incomplete houses leaning east and west, the burly, swarthy farmers in the fields, bare-chested. I have already traveled this road a few times, and this time I feel even more bored and monotonous. The lush green grass of the south, the gentle, charming waves of ponds or streams, are of course nowhere to be seen here, and a picture of severe drought is vividly presented before people's eyes. Some wheat has already turned yellow and formed kernels, but it is short, less than a foot tall; worse, it is faintly yellowish, weak and withered like autumn grass. But the sound of the orange stalks, the shadow of the waterwheel pavilion, are very rare. The drought in the north seems to be even more thorough than in the south.

When the train arrived in Tai'an, a passenger joined me in my compartment, an old man in his sixties. His deep purple-brown face, his bushy white beard, and his bright eyes, his forehead engraved with three deep wrinkles like that of the God of Longevity, were particularly attractive to me. Thinking positively, I felt he was a quaint figure from a Song or Yuan painting; thinking negatively, I saw a typical country bumpkin landlord before me. As soon as he came in, he cupped his hands to the tea attendant, cupped his hands to the ticket inspector, and cupped his hands respectfully to me. I had to greet him. After exchanging names as a matter of routine, I caught a glimpse of his rough, wrinkled hands covered in mud—I thought of a topic for conversation.

"Old gentleman, it probably hasn't rained here for a long time?"

"You can tell by looking at the wheat along the way." He puffed out his white beard, fanned himself with a paper fan printed with stone-printed calligraphy and paintings, and continued in a lively, merchant-like tone: "There hasn't been much rain since spring this year. It's been windy for the past month. Digging wells? After digging several fathoms, you still can't see a drop of water. People in the countryside have to travel dozens of miles to fetch a bucket of water. ... Is there a shortage of rain in the south too?" He turned to ask me.

"I heard that Jiangsu and Hubei are also suffering from drought."

"Oh, that's terrible. I went to Xinyangzhou in previous years, and the wheat there was half a person tall, lush green and lovely, not worried about a shortage of rain. We really don't know what we've done to offend the heavens! Moreover, if there are strong winds in the spring, there will definitely be floods in May and June. I've lived for over sixty years and experienced a lot, you wait and see!"

Although his words had a bit of a "crocodile tears" feel to them, I believed that his prediction would unfortunately come true.

After the train passed Jinan, my companion in the carriage was replaced by a middle-aged man, although also a rural landlord, but belonging to another type. He wore a set of blue silk casual clothes, tall and big, even larger than the average northerner: but all he had now was a coarse skeleton covered with a layer of skin, without much muscle. His forehead and cheekbones were sunken, and his skin was dull yellow, like a giant beast starving in a zoo. After he got on the train, he kept smoking cigarettes, occasionally chatting with me in a bland manner.

When I lay on the bunk after lunch, closing my eyes to prepare for a nap, my companion closed the door of the compartment. I opened my eyes and glimpsed him taking something out of his bag. I stared intently, and it turned out to be a hypodermic needle. My curiosity was piqued, and I kept my eyes half-closed, secretly watching what he was doing. He wiped the hypodermic needle with cotton a few times like a doctor, then turned his back to me, pulled up his trouser leg, and made a gesture of injecting his calf. After rubbing his leg for a while, he lightly wiped the hypodermic needle and hid it back in his bag.

"Is this the so-called morphine injection?" This time I had my eyes opened; no wonder this giant was just an empty shell of skin and bones. I thought to myself, but I was still a little skeptical. Later, I carefully watched him, and the many vaguely visible black spots on his arms and legs proved that my guess was correct.

Friend, what I told you last time was indeed just some trivial matters, but for you who have been away from your homeland for many years, it should still have some meaning, right? I'm about to arrive at my destination, I'll tell you more next time!

Every Time I Come Back

— Ding

Dusk descends, and as the factory whistle wails like a demon, I am liberated from the gloomy, oil-smelling, suffocating factory. After a whole day of overwork, I now have the right to breathe a mouthful of fresh air. Under the free sky, I stretch my limbs, exhale a long breath, and stagger back to my home.

When I get home, my father is still squatting on the broken-legged stool, just like yesterday, his thick eyebrows furrowed, casting a lazy glance at me with his painful, melancholic eyes. This seems like a greeting, but it also expresses some kind of request from my father. At this moment, with this tired and sorrowful heart, I nod my head silently to him, and then go straight to the corner of the room. I do this deliberately, because I dare not approach my father's side. Whenever my father sees me near him, he starts a long stream of nagging words that make me very uncomfortable. Especially when my father asks me for money to buy wine and I don't have a single penny to give him, my father immediately puts on a stern face and scolds me harshly. I know my father's temper. Since he lost his job, he likes to drink, and his personality has completely changed. Now, he spends his days either wandering the streets or sulking at home, and therefore often makes things difficult for us. But we understand the inner pain that has led to this sad behavior of my father. So we not only do not dislike him, nor do we have any hateful thoughts towards his bad behavior.

At night, when all the family members are sleeping soundly, my father quietly gets up alone. He can never sleep soundly—ever since he lost his job. In the pitch-black night, he gropes around like a cat. He knocks things over, making a loud crashing noise that awakens us. My mother often argues with my father because of this. She is very distressed and heartbroken, because both my mother and father are getting old, and like me, she has to work hard during the day and wants to rest well at night; otherwise, we will be kicked out by life. But often, when we are drifting into sleep, my father's stomach can't bear the hunger pangs anymore. After losing his job, I don't know why, but my father's stomach seems to have grown bigger, and his appetite is stronger. In short, besides feeling desolate, what else can we say about my father's unavoidable and disturbing actions? You must know: we are people living in poverty. Besides two meals a day of coarse food that can barely fill us up, we have almost nothing tasty to put in our mouths. So, there is a reason why my father is like that.

In the past, when he had a job, my father was different from now. He would get up early and tidy up the household items, arranging everything neatly, before going to work calmly. At the factory, he was very "well-behaved" and worked diligently. So he was once praised by the foreman. In the evening, when he came back, as long as he had money, my father would definitely buy some peanuts or the like for my younger siblings to eat. Sometimes he could patiently tell them some jokes and strange news he had heard from others. In short, at that time, my father was a gentle person, lived a very disciplined life, and was clearly a happy and careful person. So at that time, as long as we were all together, we would chat and laugh, and life seemed very happy.

But this joy seemed to have no connection with us, and it quickly left us and went far away. I feel that only melancholy and distress are the true companions of us poor people. It follows us closely at all times, as if our soul is in our body.

Counting from the time my father was laid off due to old age until now, it has been more than three years. Time passes by boringly, minute by minute, day by day, month by month, year by year, and my father is still idle, spending his days and nights in a kind of painful life. We don't know how to help my father pass these difficult and long years.

Soon, my mother also suffered the same misfortune. As such, our family was plunged into even greater misery and poverty. Whenever I come back from the factory, a kind of human pain assaults my heart. My father and mother often quarrel and fight over meals. Seeing this unfortunate life, I have no heart for life anymore. How can we end these days? For the disasters that are approaching us day by day, for this seemingly endless oppression, for us people living in such an environment, I deeply feel as if a sharp blade is inserted into my flesh and not pulled out, the pain is so intense.

My father is obviously much older than before, and his physique is also very hunched. A kind of gray death has shrouded his pale and haggard face. My mother, too, is sick and vomiting blood because of being angered by my father. Her difficult cough, her intermittent voice, her gloomy face filled with misfortune, her unavoidable shadow of death... My heart is simply broken, every time I come back from the factory.

Street Lamp

— Lin Hao

Night, squeezing out the blackness of ink,

Surrounding gloom,

Like being immersed in an ice cellar.

Northwest wind blowing strands of cold,

Do you, feel startled?

A demonic shadow seems stuck to your back,

Tightly and tightly;

Sudden steps cannot dispel fear,

Your heart seems about to leap out from the corner of your mouth.

In the sky, neither full nor crescent moons,

Occupying are those things twitching small eyes,

Those things laughing at your baseness,

You, roll into a cage of terror,

Unable to hear its breath,

Only complaining about this rugged path!

Walking on and on,

The demonic shadow never leaves your back,

Small eyes still laughing,

You are infuriated, your feet empty—run!

Drilling out of the dark path,

A bit of light scatters at the road corner to the right,

Ah! Should you celebrate this?

And widen your tired eyes,

Indulgently scanning:

The light kills the demonic shadow,

Takes away the smile of the small eyes,

Even hammers to death your terror,

Friend, how should you celebrate?

College Days (2)

— By German author, Storm, translated by Chen Yin Zhi

Fritz and I, we both immediately agreed to invite Lena Li, Du Lijia to be the eighth female dance partner. We naturally encountered some difficulties: because when we brought out our suggestion, those little girls and noble ladies all put on serious faces and remained silent. But the mayor's beloved son did have the ability, and pulled the mayor's wife to our side; in front of this clear-headed lady's straightforward and decisive character, those girls' frowns and her mother's obvious opposition—this was even more fierce—were all powerless.

So one afternoon we walked towards the French tailor's house. —I often regret that I broke off with the son of the carpenter who did business for my family, his sister almost came and went with little Bo Lijia girl every day: I also very much wanted to restore this friendship, and go to his father's workshop to learn carpentry; because Christopher was still a young man with self-esteem, and his mind was not simple, but he especially hated middle school students, he called them "Latins" in a disgusted tone; he often gathered a group of friends with the same aspirations on the sports field to fight those "Latins" recklessly, no matter how many times they fought, this war would not end.

But now I don't need that kind of introduction: because we have come to the front of the house, stepped on the yellow leaves of the linden tree that fell in the autumn wind, and walked to the low doorway. At the sound of the doorbell, Mrs. Bo Lijia came out from the kitchen to greet us; after wiping her hands on her white apron, she invited us into the small living room.

It is not obvious that this short, plump woman with golden hair would give birth to such a gentle and lovely black-haired girl. When we came in, this girl was putting down her work and standing up, leaning against the money counter with a feeling of half curiosity and half shyness.

When Fritz said our invitation, a red cloud appeared on her face, and I saw her eyes shine and open wide; but when her mother heard it and did not respond, and showed a thoughtful look and shook her head, she gently slipped behind her mother and walked out from the door that seemed to lead to the bedroom.

I glanced at the table she was sitting next to when she greeted us. Among the pieces of cloth and other little girl's things was a pair of Latin cloth shoes, even the edges were done, it seemed that she was just doing this thing. This pair of shoes was extremely small, and my childhood fantasy couldn't help but remind me of the pair of small feet that wore these shoes; in my mind, I seemed to see that pair of small feet already crossing with my feet in dancing, and I still wanted to ask her to stand for a while, but those feet stopped for a while, and moved for a while, constantly teasing me.

While my mind was dreaming these phantoms, Mrs. Bo Lijia was starting to ask my friend—I naturally pushed him to speak—to argue with each other, until later the mayor's wife's name was mentioned, this argument gradually inclined to our side.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Random Words

Three Solutions Proposed for Youth Problems

— Xing An

To be born as a youth in this turbulent era is truly unfortunate! Youth is originally optimistic, promising, and progressive. But now it is not like this. Today's youth is often tightly pressed by many worries and cannot help but feel the hardship of life, presenting bewilderment, regret, and despair!

Modern youth urgently need to solve many problems, and these three are the most important: academics, love, and career. These three personal issues not only put ordinary youth in a distressed situation, but sometimes even force them to commit suicide! The newspapers a few days ago reported a news item about a young man who committed suicide by taking poison because his parents refused to allow him to continue his studies. Recently, another case occurred of a university student committing suicide by throwing himself into the river due to a broken heart. This is regarding academics and love. As for those who sacrifice their lives due to unemployment, they are even more numerous!

Youth problems are overall social problems, not individual problems of youth. This is easy to understand. For example, the unemployment problem, which from the surface seems to be an individual problem, is actually a social problem. Because the current inability of a group of youth to find a way out, a sluggish society is the biggest reason. Therefore, the unemployment problem of youth is also an overall social problem. Therefore, some people advocate that youth problems cannot be solved alone. Youth problems can only be solved when overall social problems are solved. This is correct.

However, solving overall social problems is ultimately an extremely difficult task. At least in the near future, there is no way to start. So what should we do? Put the youth problem aside for the time being? If this is the case, we can only watch a group of youth, one by one, take the dangerous road! This is absolutely unacceptable. Before the overall social problems can be solved, the youth problem really has the need to be solved as an individual problem. Such a solution may not be thorough, but it is urgent!

What are the methods to solve youth problems alone? This can be divided into three aspects.

First, let's talk about academic problems. We admit that academics are very important to youth. But we must understand that the current education system in our country cannot give every youth an equal opportunity to study. Therefore, it is really difficult for a poor youth to hope to be promoted from elementary school to middle school, or from middle school to university. But this doesn't matter. It must be known that knowledge is not necessarily obtained by entering school. Diligent self-study can also achieve the purpose of seeking knowledge. There are many erudite scholars in the world whose knowledge is not obtained through school education, but through their own hard work. Moreover, the current school education in our country is also very unreliable. Why should a youth be disappointed because he cannot enter school to study?

Second, let's take the love problem. Youth love is also necessary. But modern youth must not regard love as something sacred when talking about love. It must be known that the present is a world of money, everything is commodified, and love is no exception. A poor boy will be rejected everywhere when pursuing the opposite sex. Youth should be aware of this. So if you want to fall in love, success is best, and failure is not necessary to be discouraged. If you are rejected by this one, look for another. I am not looking at love as child's play, but it is really necessary to do so. Otherwise, you can only commit suicide, there is no second way to go!

Third, let's talk about career problems. A youth must have a career in order to live. But in this era of extreme social depression, there are more people than jobs, and it is not easy to find a job. Therefore, to solve the career problem, it is best for those who have jobs to be content with their jobs and not be fickle. Those who do not have jobs, as long as there is something to do, even if the position is low, they should condescend. The important thing is to choose a career, do not hold overly extravagant hopes. This will fail. Especially a part of the educated youth with considerable education should not regard themselves too highly and regard themselves as a special class. There is no high or low in occupations. Anything that benefits the people can be done! In case of unemployment, do not be discouraged. As long as you do not have extravagant ideas, work will definitely not reject you.

In short, a modern youth who wants to free himself from his own distress should have a clear understanding of the environmental era we are in. We must recognize that in this society we should not be at the mercy of the environment, we should overcome the environment. We must rise up our own strength to make up for all the defects of society. Because the progress of a society depends on the promotion of youth!
